 1601 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      5 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0A96               | * Compiles shape data into native 65816 code that
 1602 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      6 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0A96               | * draws sprites via direct-page writes to SHR shadow RAM.
 1603 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      7 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0A96               | *
 1604 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      8 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0A96               | * Call: copy sprite table ($18 bytes) to bank $00 direct page,

 1607 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     11 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0A96               | * Sprite table format (24 bytes at DP offsets $00-$17):
 1608 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     12 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0A96               | *   $00 ADRL Rout_Adr    — output: where compiled code is written

 1610 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     14 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0A96               | *   $08 ADRL Msk_Adr     — $000000=none, $FFFF00=auto, $FEFE00=decor

 1612 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     16 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0A96               | *   $0E DA   Nb_Lgn      — bytes per shape row
 1613 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     17 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0A96               | *   $10 DA   Nb_Col      — bytes per shape column
 1614 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     18 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0A96               | *   $12 DA   Lgn         — row ($FFFF=dynamic via Y register)
 1615 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     19 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0A96               | *   $14 DA   Col         — column

 2180 |  3  Checkerboard.s      4 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0E02               | * Pre-computes 8 frames of perspective-correct checkerboard
 2181 |  3  Checkerboard.s      5 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0E02               | * into IMAGE buffer ($030000). Each frame is offset by a
 2182 |  3  Checkerboard.s      6 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0E02               | * different horizontal scroll amount.
 2183 |  3  Checkerboard.s      7 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0E02               | *
 2184 |  3  Checkerboard.s      8 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0E02               | * Uses colors $4 and $E for the two stripe colors.
 2185 |  3  Checkerboard.s      9 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0E02               | * At runtime, palette swapping between palette 0/2 on
 2186 |  3  Checkerboard.s     10 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0E02               | * alternating scanlines creates the full checkerboard effect.
